Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

017468,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
017469,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
017470,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
017471,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
017472,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
017473,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
017474,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
017475,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
017476,000011:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
017477,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017478,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
017479,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 403-484
017480,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL

017491,000026:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017492,000027:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017493,000028:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017494,000029:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017495,000030: 
017496,000031:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017497,000032: 
017498,000033:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017499,000034:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017500,000035:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017501,000036:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017502,000037:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017503,000038:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017504,000039:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017505,000040:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017506,000041:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017507,000042: 
017508,000043:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017509,000044:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017510,000045:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017511,000046:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017512,000047:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017513,000048:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017514,000049:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017549,000084: 
017550,000085:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017551,000086: 
017552,000087:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017553,000088:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017554,000089:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017555,000090:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017556,000091:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017557,000092: 
017558,000093:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017559,000094:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017560,000095:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017561,000096:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017562,000097: 
017563,000098:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017564,000099:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017565,000100:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017566,000101:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017567,000102:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017568,000103: 
017569,000104:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
017570,000105:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017571,000106:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017572,000107:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 404 

017574,000109:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017575,000110:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017576,000111:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017577,000112:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017578,000113:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017579,000114:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017580,000115:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017581,000116:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017582,000117:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017583,000118:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017584,000119: 
017585,000120:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017586,000121:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017587,000122:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017588,000123: 
017589,000124: 
017590,000125:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017591,000126: 
017592,000127:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017593,000128:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017594,000129:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017595,000130: 
017596,000131:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017597,000132:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017598,000133:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017599,000134:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017600,000135:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017601,000136:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017602,000137:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017603,000138: 
017604,000139:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017605,000140:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017606,000141: 
017607,000142: 
017608,000143:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017609,000144: 
017610,000145:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017611,000146:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017612,000147:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017613,000148:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017614,000149: 
017615,000150: 
017616,000151:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017617,000152: 
017618,000153:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017619,000154:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017620,000155:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017621,000156:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017622,000157: 
017623,000158:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 405 

017625,000160:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017626,000161: 
017627,000162: 
017628,000163:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017629,000164: 
017630,000165:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017631,000166:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
017632,000167: 
017633,000168:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017634,000169:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017635,000170:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017636,000171:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017637,000172: 
017638,000173:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017639,000174:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017640,000175: 
017641,000176:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017642,000177:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017643,000178:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017644,000179:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017645,000180: 
017646,000181:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017647,000182:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017648,000183: 
017649,000184:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017650,000185:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017651,000186: 
017652,000187:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017653,000188: 
017654,000189:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017655,000190:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017656,000191:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017657,000192:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017658,000193: 
017659,000194:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017660,000195:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017661,000196: 
017662,000197:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017663,000198:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017664,000199: 
017665,000200: 
017666,000201:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017667,000202:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017668,000203:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017669,000204:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017694,000229:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017695,000230:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017696,000231:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017697,000232:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017698,000233:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017699,000234:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017700,000235:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017701,000236:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017702,000237:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017703,000238:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017704,000239:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017705,000240:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017706,000241:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017707,000242:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017708,000243:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017709,000244:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017710,000245:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017711,000246:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017712,000247:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017713,000248:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017714,000249:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017715,000250:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1
017716,000251:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017717,000252:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER,11-13,C RELAYS
017718,000253:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017719,000254:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017720,000255:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017721,000256:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017722,000257:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017723,000258:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017724,000259:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017725,000260:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017726,000261:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017727,000262:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017728,000263:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017848,000383: 
017849,000384: 
017850,000385:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017851,000386:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017852,000387:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017853,000388:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017854,000389:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017855,000390:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017856,000391: 
017857,000392:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017858,000393:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017859,000394:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017860,000395:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017861,000396:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017862,000397:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017863,000398: 
017864,000399:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017865,000400:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
017866,000401:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
017867,000402:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
017868,000403:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
017869,000404:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
017870,000405:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
017871,000406:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
017872,000407:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
017873,000408:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
017874,000409:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
017875,000410:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017876,000411: 
017877,000412: 
017878,000413:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017879,000414: 
017880,000415:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017881,000416:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017882,000417:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017883,000418:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017884,000419:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017885,000420:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 410 

017887,000422:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017888,000423:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017889,000424:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017890,000425:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017891,000426:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017892,000427:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017893,000428:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017894,000429:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017895,000430: 
017896,000431: 
017897,000432:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017898,000433:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017899,000434:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017900,000435:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
017901,000436:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
017902,000437:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
017903,000438:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
017904,000439:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
017905,000440:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
017906,000441:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
017907,000442:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
017908,000443:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
017909,000444: 
017910,000445: 
017911,000446:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
017912,000447: 
017913,000448:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
017914,000449:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
017915,000450:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
017916,000451:

Page 426 

018626,001161:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018627,001162:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018628,001163:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018629,001164:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018630,001165:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018631,001166:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018632,001167: 
018633,001168:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018634,001169:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018635,001170: 
018636,001171:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018637,001172: 
018638,001173:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018639,001174:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018640,001175:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018641,001176: 
018642,001177:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018643,001178:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018644,001179:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018645,001180:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018646,001181:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018647,001182:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018648,001183: 
018649,001184:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018650,001185:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018651,001186:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018652,001187:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018653,001188:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018654,001189: 
018655,001190:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018656,001191:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018657,001192:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018658,001193:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018659,001194:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018660,001195:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018661,001196:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018662,001197:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018663,001198: 
018664,001199: 
018665,001200:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018666,001201:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018667,001202:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018668,001203: 
018669,001204: 
018670,001205:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018671,001206:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018672,001207: 
018673,001208:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018674,001209:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018675,001210:

Page 427 

018677,001212:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018678,001213: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018679,001214: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018680,001215: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
018681,001216: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
018682,001217: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2

Page 450 

019822,002357:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019823,002358:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019824,002359:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019825,002360:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019826,002361:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019827,002362: 
019828,002363:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019829,002364:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019830,002365:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019831,002366:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019832,002367:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019833,002368:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019834,002369:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019835,002370: 
019836,002371:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019837,002372:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019838,002373:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019839,002374: 
019840,002375:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019841,002376:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019842,002377: 
019843,002378:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019844,002379:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019845,002380: 
019846,002381:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

019973,002508:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019974,002509:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019975,002510:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
019976,002511: 
019977,002512:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019978,002513: 
019979,002514:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019980,002515:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019981,002516:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019982,002517: 
019983,002518:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019984,002519:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
019985,002520:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
019986,002521: 
019987,002522: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019988,002523: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019989,002524: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019990,002525: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
019991,002526: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
019992,002527: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
019993,002528: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
019994,002529: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019995,002530:

020421,002956:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
020422,002957:

Page 463 

020424,002959:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020425,002960: 
020426,002961:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020427,002962: 
020428,002963:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020429,002964:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020430,002965:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020431,002966:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020432,002967: 
020433,002968:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020434,002969:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020435,002970:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020436,002971: 
020437,002972:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020438,002973:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020439,002974:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020440,002975:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020441,002976:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020442,002977:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020443,002978:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020444,002979:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020445,002980:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020446,002981:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020447,002982:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020448,002983: 
020449,002984: 40,3457           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020450,002985: 40,3460           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020451,002986: 40,3461           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020452,002987: 40,3462           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020453,002988: 40,3463           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020454,002989: 40,3464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020455,002990: 40,3465           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020456,002991: 40,3466           03475                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020457,002992: 40,3467           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020458,002993: 40,3470           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020459,002994: 40,3471           03473                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020460,002995: 40,3472           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020461,002996: 40,3473           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020462,002997: 40,3474           20723                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020463,002998: 40,3475           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020464,002999: 40,3476           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020465,003000: 40,3477           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020466,003001: 40,3500           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020467,003002: 40,3501           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020468,003003: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020469,003004: 
020470,003005: 40,3503                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020471,003006:

Page 464 

020473,003008:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020474,003009:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020475,003010:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020476,003011:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020477,003012:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020478,003013: 
020479,003014:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020480,003015:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020481,003016:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020482,003017: 
020483,003018:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020484,003019:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020485,003020: 
020486,003021:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020487,003022:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020488,003023:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020489,003024:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020490,003025:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020491,003026: 
020492,003027:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020493,003028:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020494,003029:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020495,003030:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020496,003031: 
020497,003032:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020498,003033:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020499,003034:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020500,003035:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020501,003036:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020502,003037:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020503,003038:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020504,003039: 
020505,003040:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020506,003041:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020507,003042: 
020508,003043:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020509,003044:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020510,003045: 
020511,003046:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020512,003047:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020513,003048: 
020514,003049:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020515,003050:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020516,003051:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020517,003052:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020518,003053:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020519,003054:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020520,003055:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020521,003056: 
020522,003057:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 465 

020524,003059:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020525,003060:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020526,003061:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020527,003062:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020528,003063:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020529,003064:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020530,003065:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020531,003066:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020532,003067:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020533,003068: 
020534,003069:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020535,003070:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020536,003071: 
020537,003072:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
020538,003073: 
020539,003074:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020649,003184:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020650,003185:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020651,003186:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020652,003187:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020653,003188:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020654,003189: 
020655,003190: 
020656,003191:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020657,003192:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020658,003193:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020659,003194:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020660,003195:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020661,003196: 
020662,003197: 
020663,003198:                                                                                                  #  L  TO ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020664,003199:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020665,003200:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020666,003201:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020667,003202:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020668,003203:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020669,003204:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020670,003205:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020671,003206:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020672,003207:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020673,003208: 
020674,003209: 
020675,003210:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 468 

020677,003212:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020678,003213:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020679,003214:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020680,003215:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020681,003216:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020682,003217: 
020683,003218:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020684,003219:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020685,003220:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020686,003221:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020687,003222:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020688,003223:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020689,003224:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020690,003225:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020691,003226: 
020692,003227: 
020693,003228:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020694,003229: 
020695,003230: 
020696,003231:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020697,003232:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020805,003340: 
020806,003341:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY MODREG DIRECTLY. IT PUTS IN EXEC REQUEST WITH
020807,003342:                                                                                                  #  PRIO 30000 FOR DSPMMJB AND RETURNS TO CALLER.
